–¥—É–º–∞–µ—à—å –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ —Ç–∞–∫ —Ç—É—Ç ((e as { code?: string }).code === 'EEXIST' ?

  async dir_ensure() {
    if (this.dir_checked instanceof Error) throw this.dir_checked

    const dir = this.dir()
    if (this.dir_checked) return dir

    try {
      await mkdir(dir, this.mask())
      this.dir_checked = true
      return dir
    } catch (e) {
      if ((e as { code?: string }).code === 'EEXIST') {
        this.dir_checked = true
        return dir
      }

      this.dir_checked = this.err(e, { dir, action: 'dir_checked' })
      throw this.dir_checked
    }
  }

  const mixes = new WeakMap<Object, $mol_error_mix>()

  export function $gd_core_fail_normalize(
    message: string,
    cause: unknown,
    errors: Error[],
  ) {
    if ($mol_promise_like(cause)) return cause

    const mix_get = () => new $mol_error_mix(message, cause, ...errors)

    let mix
    if (cause && typeof cause === 'object') {
      mix = mixes.get(cause)
      if (! mix) mixes.set(cause, mix = mix_get())
    } else mix = $mol_wire_sync(mix_get)()

    return mix
  }

Sergey Yuferev 
  function $mol_error_cause_serialize(value: any): string {
    if (!value || typeof value !== 'object') return JSON.stringify(value)

    if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(val => $mol_error_cause_serialize(val)).join('\n')

    if (value instanceof Error) {
      return value.stack?.trim()
        .replace( /at /gm, '   at ' )
        .replace( /^(?!    +at )(.*)/gm, '    at | $1 (#)' ) ?? ''
    }

    const props = [] as string[]
    for (const key in value) {
      props.push(`${key} ${$mol_error_cause_serialize(value[key])}`)
    }

    return props.join('\n')
  }
